              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1565808293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11696081092782371109"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br/>{ARC Generously Provided by Authors}<br/><br/><br/><br/>Just FABULOUS!!<br/>I've been dying to get to this one and so happy I finally got to read it!<br/><br/><br/><b>This house is an illusion. It's polished and pretty, but the dream Callum is trying to sell is as flimsy as paper. Nothing stays shiny forever in this world.</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/6f0835d4bc151d22829509c3e8818b5f_zpshg3v7rdi.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461988311i/18939824._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 6f0835d4bc151d22829509c3e8818b5f_zpshg3v7rdi.jpg' width='340' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>When the buzz first started going around about this book months ago, I was extremely intrigued. I was told this was one hell of a book that was going to knock my socks off. <b>IT DEFINITELY DID!!</b> It</span>
  <span id="freeText11696081092782371109" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br>{ARC Generously Provided by Authors}<br><br><br><br>Just FABULOUS!!<br>I've been dying to get to this one and so happy I finally got to read it!<br><br><br><b>This house is an illusion. It's polished and pretty, but the dream Callum is trying to sell is as flimsy as paper. Nothing stays shiny forever in this world.</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/6f0835d4bc151d22829509c3e8818b5f_zpshg3v7rdi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461988311i/18939824._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6f0835d4bc151d22829509c3e8818b5f_zpshg3v7rdi.jpg" width="340" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>When the buzz first started going around about this book months ago, I was extremely intrigued. I was told this was one hell of a book that was going to knock my socks off. <b>IT DEFINITELY DID!!</b> It was compared to the tv series <i>Gossip Girl</i>. I have seen that show and it really wasn’t my cuppa. In my opinion, this book beats the hell out of Gossip Girl. Except for some of the sad things that have happened to Ella, I would say, for the most part, this is a teenage girls’ fantasy come to life.<br><br><br><br>Ella is a sixteen-year-old who has been living on her own for the past couple of years after her mother died of cancer. She has been able to keep her lack of parental guardianship a secret from the authorities and to survive, she works as a stripper in a seedy night club. The girl keeps all of her savings and belongings in a backpack that she takes with her everywhere, just in case she ever needs to go on the run at a moment’s notice. Ella has never met her father and actually has no idea who he is. One day a man appears at her school and he claims to be her legal guardian. He knows all about her mother’s death and how she has been living and supporting herself. Callum Royal tells Ella that her father has recently died and that he was named her guardian in his will. Having lived in some of the worst environments, Ella isn’t quick to trust Callum and tries to run away. She’s quickly found by Callum and he brings her back to his home to live with him and his five sons. <b> FIVE VERY ALPHA &amp; SEXY AS HELL SONS!!!</b> The Royals seem to have it all – wealth, looks, and power!! Now you see why I said this is like a girl’s dream come true????!!<br><br><br><br><br>To get Ella to agree to come back with him and stay at his place, Callum offers her $10,000 up front and promises an extra $10,000 for every month she stays. If she goes off to college, she gets $250,000, and once she graduates there is more $$$ to come!! Now who could say no to that offer??!! Certainly not Ella! But she’s definitely not a gold digger, which is what the five Royal boys all seem to think she is. They all give her a really frosty reception when she first arrives and make her life a bit hellish at the school they attend, Astor Park Prep Academy. Somehow Ella can’t help but fight this strong attraction she feels for Reed Royal, the second oldest son who has a very hot temper and seems to rule the school and the Royal clan. Reed has gotten under Ella’s skin. But she may have succeeded in affecting Reed as well.<br><br><br><br>There is a lot of drama going on with the Royal boys, Callum’s slutty girlfriend, Ella’s father’s widow, and some snobby classmates from Astor Park Prep. I loved every minute of it!! I can tell you that it was so good I read it in one day. Once you start it, you will find it hard to put down. The only problem is, we end on a big cliffy and book two isn’t out until July!! I mean that is not as bad as having to wait SIX MONTHS for <b>The Walking Dead</b> to come back on, BUT STILL!!!! I NEED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENS NEXT!!!<br><br><br><br>What is it with authors deciding to co-write books lately??!! I’ve read several just recently and they ALL were FIVE STAR reads for me!! Elle Kennedy &amp; Jen Frederick are no exception!! These two have created the most intoxicating story I have read yet!!! If you haven’t read this one, you definitely need to bump it up your TBR!! It is a book that is not to be missed!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452041283i/17638294.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1852461666?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Always Pouting" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Always Pouting" href="/user/show/48650982-always-pouting">Always Pouting</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1852461666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2142352786644973957">Apparently this is supposed to be YA and I didn't really know that until I saw other people's reviews where they were horrified after reading it. I just wanted to say though that when I was 13/14 I read fanfiction that was just as bad as this book so like it doesn't seem that strange to me that this is YA. <br/>Ella's mom dies and she works at a strip club to support herself when one day someone named Callum Royal appears to take her away from it all. She goes to live with him and his three sons in t</span>
  <span id="freeText2142352786644973957" style="display:none">Apparently this is supposed to be YA and I didn't really know that until I saw other people's reviews where they were horrified after reading it. I just wanted to say though that when I was 13/14 I read fanfiction that was just as bad as this book so like it doesn't seem that strange to me that this is YA. <br />Ella's mom dies and she works at a strip club to support herself when one day someone named Callum Royal appears to take her away from it all. She goes to live with him and his three sons in their gigantic home and soon finds out that Callum was her dad's best friend. The plot line is of course far fetched and ridiculous but I really enjoyed this book. Maybe because like I said I used to read fanficiton and this reminded me of what I used to enjoy about it. The writing isn't literature and there's a lot of sex but I enjoyed the sexual undertones as well as the romance. It was amusing and well paced story that kept me reading. I liked Ella and I enjoyed all the hijinks she gets to. I can totally get why some people may not have enjoyed it but I really enjoyed it and I really want to read the next one. It's a good pleasure read, sometimes you just want to be entertained.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1667804967" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1667804967" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1667804967?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=angst-overload">angst-overload</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=damn-this-guy-is-perfect">damn-this-guy-is-perfect</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fangirling">fangirling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=i-laughed-hard">i-laughed-hard</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=first-author-read">first-author-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1667804967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2896599423613366594"><b>5 Royal Stars!</b><br/><br/>DAMN FEELS.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465972282ra/19421968.gif' width='350' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let's just say this one quickly made it to my new favorite reads this year. <b>So absolutely freaking good!</b> I'm telling you guys, this is the kind of book that will stay glued to your hands as you race through the pages in one or two sittings. All the delightful elements, swoon factor, name it all, they're here. <br/><br/>The storyline of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28678119.Paper_Princess__The_Royals___1_' title='Paper Princess (The Royals, #1) by Erin Watt' rel='nofollow noopener'>Paper Princess</a> was a little cliché to me maybe because in my younger years I used to go gaga over <i>Boys Over Flowers</i> and <i>F4</i> and this book's story is</span>
  <span id="freeText2896599423613366594" style="display:none"><b>5 Royal Stars!</b><br><br>DAMN FEELS.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465972282ra/19421968.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's just say this one quickly made it to my new favorite reads this year. <b>So absolutely freaking good!</b> I'm telling you guys, this is the kind of book that will stay glued to your hands as you race through the pages in one or two sittings. All the delightful elements, swoon factor, name it all, they're here. <br><br>The storyline of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28678119.Paper_Princess__The_Royals___1_" title="Paper Princess (The Royals, #1) by Erin Watt" rel="nofollow noopener">Paper Princess</a> was a little cliché to me maybe because in my younger years I used to go gaga over <i>Boys Over Flowers</i> and <i>F4</i> and this book's story is pretty much similar to this Asian telenovela. <b>Ella Harper</b>'s life suddenly changed after her mother died and a billionaire showed up in her school and claimed as her new guardian. Having been used to poverty where she does everything to survive, even working part time as a stripper in a club to pay off her and her mom's needs, the sudden twist of event in her life was kind of crazy and overwhelming. And just when she thought it couldn't get any crazier, she found herself living together with the billionaire's aloof and brooding sons which are all... <i>yum</i>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"These Royals will ruin you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Meet the <s>F5</s> <b>Royal brothers</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465975111i/19422166.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Gideon, Reed, Easton, Sawyer,</b> and <b>Sebastian</b>.<br><br>If you think Ella was completely welcome to live in the Royal's mansion, you're wrong. These Royal brothers did everything in their power to send her back to where they thought she belongs. They were simply a-holes and they made her life a living hell despite all the luxurious things she was beginning to enjoy.<br><br>It didn't even stop there because stepping into her new school, <i>Astor Park</i>, meant stepping into a disaster because the spoilt little rich kids who think they live on the edge bullied her. And what's even worse, she found herself slowly falling in love with one of the Royals-- <b>Reed</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Reed Royal is the villain disguised as a pretty prince. Taking a bite out of him would be a huge mistake."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And soo I'm telling you all right now why this one was a WINNER for me:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381741013ra/5257105.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The concept was typical swoon-worthy.</b> Guilty-pleasure. Twisted in a way but still, you end up savoring it.<br><br><b>Beautifully written.</b> I am such a huge fan of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a>. When I heard that she's one of the authors of this book, I immediately added it to my tbr even without reading its synopsis. I haven't tried any <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6995972.Jen_Frederick" title="Jen Frederick" rel="nofollow noopener">Jen Frederick</a> book but after reading this, I thought I'm going to grab her works one of these days. The writing of the authors was so engaging and it simply draw me quickly to the story.<br><br><b>Well-portrayed characters.</b> All the characters were vibrant. There was just something so raw and real about them, especially Ella. I loved how kick-ass she was and how she was able to handle her situation which was not easy and how she handled the boys. I should've been nervous at some point because of all the craziness that surrounded her but I was so confident in her tough character that I did not worry for her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"My skill, if I have one, isn't dancing. It's my ability to believe that tomorrow can be a better day."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Page-turner.</b> The entertainment factor in this book was too much. You can't help yourself from devouring it until you're finished. No dull moments. Heck, every little detail was so exciting!<br><br><b>Sexy banters and romantic and steamy scenes.</b> There was 100% chemistry between the characters and a lot of sexual tension and it helped built up those scenes. Plus, the banters were so fun and hilarious! The authors really know how to tastefully write scenes that can make you grin. And the emotions the characters presented... they're right down to the bones.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Maybe another time, away from this place, you and me would have a different story."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The ending, however, was a huge CLIFFHANGER. But I don't consider it a drawback despite my freak-out fest after reading it. lol<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412889823ra/11437312.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are a guilty-pleasure reader, staaahp what you are doing and read this book already while I am here.... eagerly waiting. Waiting for the second book.<br><br>(I buddyread this book together with my lovely friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3047938-rachmi" rel="nofollow noopener">Rachmi</a>)<br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="2896599423613366594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1583687048?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=arc">arc</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=angsty-intense">angsty-intense</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1583687048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6494035497032753389"><i> On sale! 99 cents <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/2w5aaoL'>http://amzn.to/2w5aaoL</a> <br/>8/23/17 </i><br/><br/><b> 5 stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “No one wants to be ruined. We all want to be saved.” </i> </b><br/><br/><b> OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431167329ra/14797771.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Where do I even start? Well obviously from my rating I absolutely loved this book. When I saw the blurb I was intrigued and immediately requested the arc. Plus Elle Kennedy is a co-author and she has <i> NEVER </i> let me down. I’ve loved everything I’ve read by her so far. I’m a bit new to Erin Watt (Jen Frederick) and haven’t read any of her books, but I’ll be sure </span>
  <span id="freeText6494035497032753389" style="display:none"><i> On sale! 99 cents <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2w5aaoL">http://amzn.to/2w5aaoL</a> <br>8/23/17 </i><br><br><b> 5 stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “No one wants to be ruined. We all want to be saved.” </i> </b><br><br><b> OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431167329ra/14797771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where do I even start? Well obviously from my rating I absolutely loved this book. When I saw the blurb I was intrigued and immediately requested the arc. Plus Elle Kennedy is a co-author and she has <i> NEVER </i> let me down. I’ve loved everything I’ve read by her so far. I’m a bit new to Erin Watt (Jen Frederick) and haven’t read any of her books, but I’ll be sure to remedy that very soon.<br><br>Paper Princess is about a teenage girl named Ella, who after the passing of her mother has been living on her own. Deceiving her high school and working multiple jobs her only goal is to get a diploma so she can continue on to college. One day a man appears at her school, claiming to be a friend of her recently deceased father (a man she never knew) and saying he is now her legal guardian.<br><br>Ella is grudgingly taken to Callum Royal’s home where she is to live. Callum makes a deal with her that she cannot refuse and a part of the agreement was for her to stay in his home with his five sons. Five sons who are not at all happy to see Ella. From rags to riches Ella does her best to catch her bearings and adjust to an entirely new life. But despite wanting to remain overlooked she is constantly hurdled into the attentions of her peers, and she can either take it, or fight back.<br><br><b> <i> “No matter what Callum says or tried to do, I’m never going to be a Royal.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/Blogging%20images/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456556813i/18248686.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I say I loved this book, it is an understatement. This is a book you stay up until 3am to finish and end up feeling tired but happy the next day because it was so worth it. There was not one moment when I was bored or wanted to skim, I was completely absorbed in it until the very end. I loved being in Ella’s head and sharing her experiences with her. She’s a strong female character who doesn’t need or want saving, but in this book she realizes it doesn’t hurt to accept help from others. Ella also recognizes the value in hard work and doesn’t shirk away from jobs that others see as below themselves. She doesn’t apologize for who she is either. I found her to be a very admirable character, refreshing from all of the weak heroines we see flooding the genre. <br><br>All of the Royal boys have me intrigued, I really hope that some get their own book (like Easton and the twins). There’s so much going on and I would have loved the perspective of some of them while reading. Now Ella and Reed: my goodness someone get me a fan because their chemistry was off the charts!!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458526477ra/18497655.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I am shipping these two so hard right now!!!! I loved them together, whether they were fighting or you know, other stuff. Good stuff ;-)<br><br><br><b> <i> “I can’t decide what I like more. The calm Royal household with the voiceless Reed or the one where he’s yelling at me to stay away and threatening me with his penis.” </i> </b><br><br>Anyway if you didn’t get it by now I loved this book. This book has a very Tijan feel to it, and those who loved the Fallen Crest series will love this story. Warning! There is a very large cliffhanger at the end that I may need to join a support group to get over. But, I still think you should read this book despite the cliffhanger because I think it’s totally worth it. <br><br>And I do want to clarify, while this book is about high school students/young adults, it is not a young adult book due to language and adult content. So don't be handing it to a sixteen year old to read. Save it for when they hit college and hand it to them then!<br><br><i> ARC kindly provided by authors in exchange for an honest review </i><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/Blogging%20images/RRR.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455783307i/18148833._SX540_.png" alt=" photo RRR.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1586554536" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1586554536" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1586554536?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1586554536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12418833067664591535">Erin Watt is the brainchild of two of my fave authors in NA right now: Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick. So when I heard they're writing releasing a "cracktastic" book, I was like...<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=317czd4' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459106778i/18571013._SX540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Four hours and a cliffhanger later....<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=1z6ba1g' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459106778ra/18571014.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>A word of warning. Do not read this book if you have something important to do the next day, like go to work or go to school or just doing something that needs you to be alert and awake because you're gonna fail at it. Hard. And all because of this book. <br/><br/>Paper Princess is o</span>
  <span id="freeText12418833067664591535" style="display:none">Erin Watt is the brainchild of two of my fave authors in NA right now: Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick. So when I heard they're writing releasing a "cracktastic" book, I was like...<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=317czd4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459106778i/18571013._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Four hours and a cliffhanger later....<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=1z6ba1g" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459106778ra/18571014.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A word of warning. Do not read this book if you have something important to do the next day, like go to work or go to school or just doing something that needs you to be alert and awake because you're gonna fail at it. Hard. And all because of this book. <br><br>Paper Princess is one of the most addicting books I've read in a while. It's pure fantasy, pure fun and pure unadulterated cracktastic read. <br><br>Set in a very privilege world of the rich and the insanely rich, Paper Princess follows a story of a young high school girl named Ella who, at the start of the book was struggling to get through her life. She just lost her mother and she's been on her own trying to finish high school. Fate intervened in the form of Callum Royal. A man claiming to be Ella's biological dad's best friend and Ella guardian. Suddenly, Ella finds herself in the middle of the Royal world, which includes Callum's five young sons, one of whom caught Ella's attention immediately.<br><br>The Royals are rich, privileged and entitled. They're not really good people. They're amoral but they are also utterly fascinating. They have skeletons in their closets and you can't help but question their motives all the time especially Reed Royal, the Royal brothers' de facto leader and all around asshole. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=ofx2ev" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459106778ra/18571015.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh my gosh. This guy just pushes all of Ella's buttons even the ones she doesn't want pushed. They have insane chemistry and hate-lust going on, which is one of the most addicting factors in this book. I'm not gonna lie. There were times in the books where I want so bad to knee him in the balls. Normally, I would hate a hero like Reed because he is just horrible sometimes but because Ella was no wilting flower and has no intention of laying down and letting Reed or any Royal for that matter, walk all over her, made the story more interesting to me. <br><br>All the Royal brothers have their own personalities and little ticks and secrets that you want to uncover. I am so hoping that the authors are going to give each brothers a book because I would totally read all of them! But I'm getting ahead of myself. <br><br>As much as I loved reading about the Royals and can't help but be fascinated by them, the main attraction or the main character that keeps me glued to its pages was Ella. This girl slays. She's the perfect combination of vulnerability and toughness. And she's not afraid to stand up to the Royals and their friends who look down on her. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqs684" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459106778ra/18571016.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Paper Princess is her story. And it is only the beginning. I cannot wait for the second book to come out. And as much as I loathed that cliffhanger, there is no way to fit everything in just one book. There is still too much to uncover about the Royals, about Ella's biological dad, about Callum...everything. And I really, really want to know more about the Royal boys. <br><br>So if you're in mood for a crazy addicting story, I would highly, highly recommend this book. Yes, it's tag as YA but honestly, I wasn't bothered by the age of the characters even with the stuff that's been happening. I was too caught up in the story. It was that addicting. <br><br><i>ARC provided by Erin Watt in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_1579473518" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1579473518" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1579473518?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1579473518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16606042166084416048"><b>
  <i>”You’re a Royal now.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571264748i/28304917.png' width='430' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>…and the cheese stands alone. <br/><br/>This story simply never got me to the point where I felt like I was enjoying it. It’s in the vein of the <i>The Prince and the Pauper</i> story but with rich spoiled mean teens and felt like one big cliché. Even when the heroine’s love interest is clear and his feelings seem similar for her I was confused by what she found so attractive about him. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Smile, I beg silently at him. Smile at me. Touch me. Kiss me. Anything."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445646757ra/16685088.gif' width='430' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story felt like drama</span>
  <span id="freeText16606042166084416048" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”You’re a Royal now.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571264748i/28304917.png" width="430" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>…and the cheese stands alone. <br><br>This story simply never got me to the point where I felt like I was enjoying it. It’s in the vein of the <i>The Prince and the Pauper</i> story but with rich spoiled mean teens and felt like one big cliché. Even when the heroine’s love interest is clear and his feelings seem similar for her I was confused by what she found so attractive about him. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Smile, I beg silently at him. Smile at me. Touch me. Kiss me. Anything."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445646757ra/16685088.gif" width="430" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story felt like drama for the sake of drama occurring page after page. The plot devices were nothing special but the cliff and the uncovering of all these Royal’s secrets maybe possibly enough for me to try the next book who knows.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492139115ra/22486300.gif" width="430" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have read an awful lot of YA and these characters are supposed to be juniors in high school is laughable. As a mom of a seventeen year old junior, I’m sad to inform you that this age group doesn’t speak like this at all. Perhaps if this was a college setting it would have been more fitting for the descriptions, actions and dialogue for this group of characters. Also, the ecstasy/cocaine scene was completely off the mark and her reactions to the drug far fetched. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492139115ra/22486299.gif" width="430" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Easton Royal and the heroine are the only characters that I did actually care for. I would recommend this story for audiences eighteen years and older and not younger.<br><br><b>
  <i>”My life is mine. I live it. I control it.”</i>
</b><br></span>

<div id="review_2164980439" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2164980439" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2164980439?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Melanie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/7345713-paloma-the-romance-queen">Paloma *The Romance Queen* </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=erotic-scenes">erotic-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2164980439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9530057990335006280">I was having a rough two days mental health wise, so I just wanted to drop everything on my TBR and read something I didn’t really have to think about, but I knew I’d probably enjoy. I wanted something fast paced, with an addicting story, and maybe some sexy times, and <i>Paper Princess</i> was the perfect pick for me. <br/><br/>By looking at some of my friends’ reviews I feel like I really need to say that <b>this is not a YA book in the slightest!</b> This is NA and has a lot of sexual scenes that should only be read</span>
  <span id="freeText9530057990335006280" style="display:none">I was having a rough two days mental health wise, so I just wanted to drop everything on my TBR and read something I didn’t really have to think about, but I knew I’d probably enjoy. I wanted something fast paced, with an addicting story, and maybe some sexy times, and <i>Paper Princess</i> was the perfect pick for me. <br /><br />By looking at some of my friends’ reviews I feel like I really need to say that <b>this is not a YA book in the slightest!</b> This is NA and has a lot of sexual scenes that should only be read by mature audiences. This has many erotic scenes and for sure should have a sexual content warning. <br /><br />As for <b>trigger warnings</b>: losing a parent, underage sexual content (17), physical abuse, sexual assault, attempted rape, underage drinking, drug use, addiction, a lot of slut shaming, and a lot of toxic male masculinity. So please use caution before going into this book.<br /><br />And there are a lot of weird gender role expectations in this book, too. Like, the main female protagonist has to cook spaghetti because they boys can’t figure it out. And then, later, she can’t figure out the football teams, but she brings up the lion on the helmet. There are more of these instances sprinkled throughout the book, and I wasn’t offended, it just feels… not so great reading. <br /><br />Also, because I know most of you follow me for my fantasy reviews, I always feel it necessary to state that <b>I rate erotic books differently than other books!</b> I know many of the relationships are toxic and problematic and I completely understand that they wouldn’t be the healthiest and/or most ideal of starts for people in real life, but I love steamy reads and I rate them purely off my enjoyment, and I truly did enjoy <i>Paper Princess</i>. <br /><br /><i>Paper Princess</i> is cowritten by Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick under the pseudonym Erin Watt. And Elle Kennedy has written one of my favorite NA series of all time, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1218730524" rel="nofollow noopener">the Off-Campus series</a>, so I knew I had to eventually try out this series, too. And I’m so happy that I finally did. <br /><br />And <i>Paper Princess</i> stars a young girl named Ella, who has only known a life of jumping from new city to new city where her and her mom can barely make ends meet. But after her mother’s death, Ella is trying to survive on her own. And all she wants to do is get a high school diploma, so she can go to college and eventually give herself a stable life. <br /><br />Then, a man appears out of nowhere, claiming to be her mystery father’s best friend and business partner. He promises to give Ella a better life, because her father, too, has tragically just passed away.<br /><br />Ella is then thrown into the Royal family, where the man that is trying to help her also has five sons himself. And let’s just say that they are not the most open to the idea of their father taking in a random girl. And they all basically just think the absolute worst of Ella, right off the bat.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You may have lost your family, but you’re not alone anymore, Ella. You’re a Royal now.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Ella is quickly thrown into the world of prep schools and old money, while she is dealing with the grief of losing her mother, and the hope of starting a better life. <br /><br />I’m not going to say this book is perfect, it’s far from it, but I read this in one sitting because I truly just couldn’t put it down. The romance is amazing, the angst is out of this world, and I’m just a sucker for a good hate to love relationship and this one doesn’t disappoint. <br /><br />Also, I need to start <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2164983706" rel="nofollow noopener">Broken Prince</a> immediately, because <i>Paper Princess</i> ends on maybe the worst cliffhanger I’ve ever read in my entire life. <br /><br /><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9530057990335006280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1671776843" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1671776843" />
    <a title="Helen 2.0" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39575951-helen-2-0"><img alt="Helen 2.0" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460553725p2/39575951.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1671776843?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helen 2.0" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helen 2.0" href="/user/show/39575951-helen-2-0">Helen 2.0</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39575951-helen-2-0?shelf=read-16">read-16</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1671776843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1753383195968874204">Imagine the movie <a href='http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0377092/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mean Girls</a>. We've all watched it, right? It's a classic.<br/>Now reimagine it as an R-rated movie with smut galore.<br/>Now give all the mean girls dicks and a sexist attitude. <br/>Enter Ella, a modern Cinderella forced into stripping for money. <br/><b>Put it all together and you've got Paper Princess.</b><br/><br/>Paper Princess is fun, feisty, addicting and entertaining as all hell. It revolves around Ella the high schooler and part-time stripper. Her mother died a few years ago, leaving her to work and move a</span>
  <span id="freeText1753383195968874204" style="display:none">Imagine the movie <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0377092/" rel="nofollow noopener">Mean Girls</a>. We've all watched it, right? It's a classic.<br>Now reimagine it as an R-rated movie with smut galore.<br>Now give all the mean girls dicks and a sexist attitude. <br>Enter Ella, a modern Cinderella forced into stripping for money. <br><b>Put it all together and you've got Paper Princess.</b><br><br>Paper Princess is fun, feisty, addicting and entertaining as all hell. It revolves around Ella the high schooler and part-time stripper. Her mother died a few years ago, leaving her to work and move around constantly to try to make a living and a future for herself. Then Callum Royal shows up, claiming to be the best friend of Ella's unknown father and assuming guardianship of her. She is whisked away to his palace mansion, where she starts school with Callum's five megalomaniac narcissistic sons. <br><br><b>Let's take a look at the characters, with corresponding gifs!<br>Ella Harper:</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471906713ra/20123302.gif" height="150" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Idol Queen. Slays regularly. Doesn't take shit from anyone, especially not the Royal family (<i>excepting Reed cause she's putty in his hands</i>). When girls try to bully her for her poor background, she kicks some ass - I mean literally. <br><b>Reed Royal:</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471906692ra/20123297.gif" height="170" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Total hot stuff, runs the school; he can even issue "decrees" concerning the student body's behavior towards certain people. Honestly, I found Reed overly broody, bordering on sketchy. This is not the kind of guy you start a healthy relationship with.<br><b>Easton Royal:</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424299508ra/13742300.gif" height="150" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Not to be slut shaming but DAMN this boy gets around. Bit of a sexist pig, but he's still my uncontested favorite Royal! Easton has a sweet side to him.<br><b>Callum Royal:</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471906692ra/20123298.gif" height="150" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I don't know what's worse: his drinking problem, his failures as a parent, his blatant PDA with his girlfriend, or the way he throws around money like it's chicken feed.<br><b>The Twins:</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471906693ra/20123299.gif" height="220" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>No comment on their "sharing" habits.<br><b>Val:</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471906693ra/20123300.gif" height="160" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ideal best friend. Knows all the gossip but doesn't get sucked into all the high school evil and drama that surrounds her. Val knows what's up.<br><br>I loved the book but kind of saw the ending coming. Nevertheless I'm slide-to-the-floor relieved that Book 2 is already out and I don't have to wait for it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1753383195968874204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2108248415" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2108248415" />
    <a title="TS" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8143165-ts"><img alt="TS" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517773063p2/8143165.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2108248415?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TS" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TS" href="/user/show/8143165-ts">TS</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8143165-ts?shelf=to-the-trash-you-go">to-the-trash-you-go</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8143165-ts?shelf=1-star">1-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8143165-ts?shelf=yikes">yikes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8143165-ts?shelf=fuck-me-up-plots-and-plot-twists">fuck-me-up-plots-and-plot-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8143165-ts?shelf=overhyped">overhyped</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2108248415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12420682172997540616"><b> What the fuck did I just read? </b><br/><br/>Like this is a joke, right? <br/><br/>This book was so frustrating in so many different ways and degrees that I'm not sure how I'll be able to write a coherent review for this utter piece of shit. But I'll try.<br/><br/>Let's start with the most glaring fault in this book imo: Erin Watt's writing is fucking trash. It's so bad that I'm convinced that's why she took on a pseudonym; it's because she doesn't want people she personally knows to realize that she, an adult, who probably pas</span>
  <span id="freeText12420682172997540616" style="display:none"><b> What the fuck did I just read? </b><br><br>Like this is a joke, right? <br><br>This book was so frustrating in so many different ways and degrees that I'm not sure how I'll be able to write a coherent review for this utter piece of shit. But I'll try.<br><br>Let's start with the most glaring fault in this book imo: Erin Watt's writing is fucking trash. It's so bad that I'm convinced that's why she took on a pseudonym; it's because she doesn't want people she personally knows to realize that she, an adult, who probably passed basic high school level English, is so much of a bad writer that a middle-schooler could probably form more articulate and eloquent sentences than she can. It legit read like the Justin Bieber wattpad story my 13 year old cousin asked me to read so that she could get more views on her chapters. <br><br>Now for the more specific faults:<br><br>First of all, <i> what the actual fuck was the plot</i> in this novel, because I'm still confused? I get the premise in general: poor girl goes to live with rich man, rich man's children don't like her for no logical reason. Ok. Fair enough. But beyond that, <b>what the hell happened???</b> This was such a mess. It seemed like Watt brought forth not <i>one</i> love triangle, but <i>two</i> love triangles in which 2/3 of the characters in both love triangles were the same. So it was like 2 <i> consecutive </i> love triangles? But that's not even what annoyed me most! What frustrated me to no fucking end was that this shitty author realized her love triangles were half assed after about 30 pages of developing them and so she nipped one in the bud, only to bring forth <i>another</i> love triangle and do the same again because this bitch lacked the creativity to follow her ideas through, but also severely lacked in editors to tell her she should just cut that shit off from her book completely if she's not going to follow through with it. It was a fucking disaster. <br><br>And aside from those shitty overall plot points, this book, being a contemporary or whatever, was so <b>unrealistic</b>. Like fucking hell, it deserves its own category of books called "Wishful thinking gone wrong" because this bitch was a pauper turned into the 21st century version of a "princess", out of nowhere?? Only because she's the illegitimate love child of a guy who never cared enough to meet her, not even once? And like seriously, who is <i>actually</i> able to control the actions and choices of their siblings and the whole student body the way that our main love interest does? you don't even see that shit done by jocks in 80-90's teen movies. I had such a hard time believing aspects of this book being real life events that could potentially occur that I started to laugh out loud--not because the book was funny like it's meant to be at times, but because of what a horrible life decision the author made when choosing to write this catastrophe. Seriously, Watt should donate all the proceeds of this book to the Hurricane Harvey cause only because it would be the only way to lower the calamity that is this wretched disaster.<br><br>I'm writing this review furiously tapping on my keyboard because of how frustrated this book made me, and I'm actually worried I might need to make an appointment with the Apple Store today following this next part of the review because some letters will most likely be broken off from the sheer force and momentum of my anger punching through the keys while I write about the fucking piece of shit asshole that is supposed to be the love interest in this novel. <br><br>Fucking Reed. <br><br><b>Has there ever been a more vile love interest in a book series ever?</b> I highly doubt it. Name me a single one and I'll pity you for going through a shitstorm worse than this douche. <br><br>I get that this was supposed to be a hate-to-love relationship. That's fucking fine; in fact, they're my favorite type of contemporaries/NA/smutty reads. But there's a way to do it <i>right</i> and this was on the complete opposite spectrum of that way. <br><br>Especially in the beginning, every time Reed talked, I wanted to gouge my eyes out. He was a <i>dreadful</i> human being. We're first introduced to him barging in to Ella's room--<i>after she explicitly told him not to because she's not decent</i>--because he "doesn't <i>care</i>". WTF. NO SERIOUSLY WTF. WHAT THE ACTUAL FUCK???????????????????? And he only gets worse! That's the worst part! He slut-shames her constantly, and puts her down, and makes her feel unwelcomed at the school and at her new home, and <i>blames</i> her for being a gold-digger and sleeping with his dad (when she's not??? and he has no proof to go by that she's doing this???), and bullies her and makes his brothers and <i>the whole student body</i> bully her, and orders her around, and she's still down for him??? We're still supposed to root for them??? We're meant to like this metaphorical human garbage of a person???? Fuck that shit. That's fucked up.<br><br>And as an encore for his ultimate douchebaggery, ponder on this: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ella, our protagonist, has been drugged at a party with Molly and cocaine and God knows what else so that this rando guy she's kinda/sorta/not really seeing could take advantage of her because <i>duh, </i>she's a slut (and who perpetuated that fucking label on her in the first place anyway?? If you guessed the epitome of the piece of shit emoji but with a sad face instead of a smiley one, Reed, then you guessed right!). Predictably, our not-so-beloved Reed, saves the day. Hurray! You've done something right! But then, WHAT DOES THIS BITCH ASS BOY HAVE THE AUDACITY TO DO??!?!?!? Ella, being high and all, feels horny, and she has this unexplainable crush on Reed and wants to do shit with him. And so she tells him. Sanely, Reed tells her no, she's not in her right mind, she's fucked up right now. And he's right, she is, she's fucking drugged and has just been through the traumatic experience of almost getting raped. BUT THEN SOMEHOW THEY STILL DO SHIT???? AND THEN THIS FUCKING VILE SPECIMEN OKAYS HIS BEHAVIOUR BECAUSE <i>HE'S</i> THE ONE GIVING THE ORAL SEX? AND THEN HE HAS THE FUCKING <i>NERVE</i> TO ASK HER THE FOLLOWING DAY WHETHER WHAT HE DID WAS OKAY AND WAS IT CONSENSUAL, WHEN THIS WHOLE TIME, THIS WHOOOOOLE TIME GUYS, HE KNEW WHAT HE WAS DOING WAS SKETCHY BUT IGNORED IT (LIKE HE REPEATEDLY MENTIONS THIS)? Fuck youuuuuuuuuu. Fuck you very much.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504280856i/23739715._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like fuck. You can't make this shit up.<br><br>Reed kind of redeems himself towards the end and suddenly becomes a semi-good guy, but horrendously enough, even then, he's <b>insufferable</b>. The piece of shit is more undecided on whether he should act on his feelings and attractions towards Ella than on how undecided I get on whether I should wear one black t-shirt over another black t-shirt to school on any given day. <br><br><b>Actual summary of the last 100 pages of this book:</b><br><br><b>Reed:</b> *hooking up with Ella* This is the last time we're doing this. We can't be doing this because of hugely invalid reason that makes no sense.<br>- next night -<br><b>Reed:</b> *hooking up with Ella* This is the last time.<br>- next night -<br><b>Reed:</b> Ok but seriously this one is the last time I solemnly swear<br>- five centuries later -<br><b>Reed:</b>*plays Taylor Swift's Last Time but doesn't mean it*<br><br>Literally his attitude towards hooking up with Ella is a direct parallel to how I act when I'm thinking of going to the gym [<i>Ok I'll work out tomorrow!</i> I've been saying every day unconvincingly for the past 7 years.]<br><br>Also this is minimal but at one point he starts out of nowhere calling her 'baby' which is uncalled for because at this point, they still haven't done anything with each other and are not together, and that pet name already makes me cringe when used by a guy so I just felt like barfing at that point and was seriously tempted to go and get some Gravol for myself. And I'm still confused as to what caused him to start actually <i>liking</i> Ella? Because absolutely nothing drastic changes in their circumstances for him to suddenly start liking her? It's hella dumb. <br><br>um what else??? this book is such a huge display of fuckery that I actually have to think about what all the bad things are because the list is impossibly endless.<br> <br>oh YeAH fucking Ella. I'm going to ignore the fact that Ella's into Reed because if you want to be treated like you're the scum of the earth and get turned on by that, even though you yourself literally <i>acknowledged</i> that said person treats you as if you are no better than a fucking spider not paying the rent in a human household, than that's your prerogative. <b>But her characterization? My g0D.</b> You're telling me that this person has experienced abandonment from their biological father, the loss of a mother to cancer at a young age, extreme poverty, abuse and harrassment from her mother's various boyfriends, an underage career as a stripper, social isolation, harassment from her peers and the people fucking living with her, potential rape, and yet, she has <i>no issues</i> whatsoever? You're telling me she doesn't suffer from any form of PTSD, that she doesn't suffer from an other mental disorder, that she doesn't partake in any form of high-risk behaviour or has any social development issues, when this is unfortunately and tragically the reality of most people who suffer from at least one of those similar traumatic life events? Like there's being resilient, and then there's this. Which is basically, a "let's throw a bunch of shit at our MC to give the impression that she's three-dimensional and has a tragic backstory but fail to explore any of those harmful or triggering themes bcuz I'm not down and a douchebag is being his regular-ol'-douchebaggery-self-to-me-and-it's-getting-me-hot-and-bothered" mindset.<br><br>Also to make things even worse (like how is that even possible at this point??? if you've reached this far into the review i seriously applaud you), there's a shitton of girl-on-girl hate and slut-shaming and ISN'T THAT JUST THE <b> BEST? :) :) :) :) </b> fucking die. fuck you.<br><br>Also, somehow, this book, that is written by a <i>woman</i>, sexualises typical women behaviour and perpetuates the idea that girl-on-girl-anything = erotic for boys so you should do it for that sole reason. physically fighting with a girl? sexy. dancing up on a girl? sexy. (which don't get me wrong, you should dance with your girlfriends however you please, but <i>you shouldn't do it for a guy ogling at you and dehumanizing you</i>). Also they were dancing in cages to get the attention from boys and took <i>pride</i> in it???? Like that is the literal definition of oppression being a direct result of the objectification of women? <b>How was it a woman that wrote this anti-feminist bullshit of a manifesto?</b><br><br>I don't know what else to say except to repeat myself yet again on the fact that this was shit.<br><br>OH. And there's a cliffhanger at the end which basically just reinforces the fact that these shitty characters are shitty people and this cliffhanger is essentially there to try to convince you to not listen to your instincts that tell you to RUN AWAY FROM THIS SEQUEL because cliffhanger guise omg!!111!1. <br><br><s>Like honestly can someone who actually liked this book or didn't but dared to read the rest tell me what happens because I'm not spending more of my valuable money or time on this? </s><br><br>Overall sentiments regarding this book: I wanted to throw away this book across the room so many times but I couldn't because I read it on my Kindle and that made me sad because this book deserves destruction and I hope that one day future me will be able to suppress the traumatizing memory of having read this treachery to English literature.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1565644390" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1565644390" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1565644390?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1565644390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10035116582668749314"><b>NOW LIVE!</b> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1qkoZzP'>http://amzn.to/1qkoZzP</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458483175i/18493262._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Where to begin???? Paper Princess was like Cruel Intentions, Gossip Girl, and some crazy ass soap opera all mixed into one. AND I LOVED IT! Angst and drama galore! If you're looking for a read with:<br/><br/>-Revenge plots<br/>-Sex and lust and hate<br/>-Crazy high school drama <br/>-Family secrets<br/>-A feisty heroine who falls for her kinda/sorta step brother who is a total asshole when he's not being sexy as all hell <br/><br/>...then this right here is it. Take note though - this has been marked as</span>
  <span id="freeText10035116582668749314" style="display:none"><b>NOW LIVE!</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1qkoZzP">http://amzn.to/1qkoZzP</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458483175i/18493262._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where to begin???? Paper Princess was like Cruel Intentions, Gossip Girl, and some crazy ass soap opera all mixed into one. AND I LOVED IT! Angst and drama galore! If you're looking for a read with:<br><br>-Revenge plots<br>-Sex and lust and hate<br>-Crazy high school drama <br>-Family secrets<br>-A feisty heroine who falls for her kinda/sorta step brother who is a total asshole when he's not being sexy as all hell <br><br>...then this right here is it. Take note though - this has been marked as YA/NA. And while majority of the main characters are in their teens, TRUST me when I say the situations in here are more along Rated R territory. <br><br>So what's the crazy world of the Royals all about?<br><br>Ella is living on her own after her mother passing away and never having known her father. To support herself along with saving up for college, she is forced to resort to stripping and dancing for money. Did I mention Ella is 17? Yep. A TEENAGER taking care of herself and doing whatever she can to survive. <br><br>Insert Callum Royal, best friend to Ella's deceased father. Once he learns of Ella's existence, he makes it his mission to take her under his wing and treat her as the daughter he never had. But Callum's 5 sons, (Gideon, Reed, Easton, Sebastian and Sawyer) are NOT having it. They all believe Ella comes to live with them for more scandalous reasons and make it <i>their</i> mission to make her so uncomfortable she is forced to leave. <br><br>Reed, the second oldest at 18 and pretty much the leader of the boys (and his entire school), takes a special interest in Ella. And by special interest, I mean he totally tries to hate her but winds up wanting in her pants. <br><br><b>
  <i>...he pulls out and glides a hand over my thigh. "I'm going to make this feel so good for you."<br>"I already feel good," I protest, drawing up my legs.<br>A cocky, familiar grin shines up at me.<br>"You haven't seen anything yet."</i>
</b><br><br>Yep. I love an 18 year old named Reed Royal and I don't care if you're judging me. Go ahead. Because once you read about this boy you'll be a part of the Reed Fan Club right along side me. <br><br>But does he really care for Ella? Is he using her as a pawn in some grand scheme? YOU JUST DON'T KNOW!<br><br><b>
  <i>"The apple is dangling in front of me, juicy red and delicious, but, like the fairy tale, Reed Royal is the villain disguised as a pretty prince. Taking a bite out of him would be a huge mistake."</i>
</b><br><br>Andddddddddddd then that's when all the crazy starts to happen. Between the lust-filled moments, the revenge, and the twists, my head was spinning! Once I finished, my mind was reeling with theories, trying to figure out who is in on what, what everyone's motives really are, who's lying, who's being set up. And I am STILL thinking about it. I loved every single character in this (I didn't forget you Easton. You stole my heart!), both good and evil.<br><br>Be warned: This does end on a cliffhanger that caused me to almost throw my kindle across the room. I immediately messaged a friend where we began to swap theories on what the hell is going on for almost an hour. It was that good and it will suck you in just as much, I can guarantee it. <br><br>This was such an amazing start to what will definitely be an incredible series. I just know I will be thinking about this non-stop until the second book is out. <br><br>ADD THIS DRAMA FILLED BABY TO YOUR TBR NOW. <br><br>For a sneak peek at a few sample chapters of Paper Princess :<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.wattpad.com/story/66141169-paper-princess">https://www.wattpad.com/story/6614116...</a><br><br>Short book trailer I made:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/videos/vb.237477603070333/621310571353699/?type=2&amp;theater">https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorl...</a><br><br>Paper Princess is out NOW!<br> <br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448478009i/17148043._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Find Me On:<br><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a></span>

<div id="review_1580347956" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1580347956" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1580347956?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=advanced-copy">advanced-copy</a>,
