        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1580347956" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15423434665355476281"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430777274i/14761419.png' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> Paper Princess <br/><b>Series:</b> The Royals #1<br/><b>Author:</b> Erin Watt (Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick)<br/><b>Release date: </b> April 4, 2016<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> Yes<br/><b>HEA</b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458226739i/18459241._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book surprised the hell out of me. I'm just going to put that out there right from the start. I knew that this was written by two of my most trusted authors, so I was willing to give this book a chance regardless of what the blurb was. But I didn't know how this would completely draw me in from page one. <br/><br/>There were sever</span>
  <span id="freeText15423434665355476281" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430777274i/14761419.png" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> Paper Princess <br><b>Series:</b> The Royals #1<br><b>Author:</b> Erin Watt (Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick)<br><b>Release date: </b> April 4, 2016<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> Yes<br><b>HEA</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458226739i/18459241._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book surprised the hell out of me. I'm just going to put that out there right from the start. I knew that this was written by two of my most trusted authors, so I was willing to give this book a chance regardless of what the blurb was. But I didn't know how this would completely draw me in from page one. <br><br>There were several things about the story that would have normally made me pause before requesting a copy. Not only is it YA (which I rarely read), it has the type of hero that doesn't always work for me. Just my personal preference, I know a lot of readers go for the asshole hero every time, but I'm very, very picky when it comes to that. These authors weaved their magic for me because they made me addicted and desperate for more of Ella and Reed's love/hate <s>war</s> relationship.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458229151i/18459732.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> What made me accept Reed's attitude and behavior? A combination of the spellbinding writing and the heroine who doesn't take one ounce of his shit. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458229151i/18459733.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <i>loved</i> this girl. <b>LOVED</b> For every hit he tried to make with her, she hit back just as hard, or harder. She's seen more struggle and tragedy than most people see in a lifetime. And it's made her tough-a fighter. Living in the Royal's house and inner circle, it's a life skill that she desperately needs. <br><br>Ella comes to live with Reed when his father becomes her guardian. She never knew her father, and her mother recently passed away from cancer. She's an (underage) ex-stripper, supporting herself through high school trying to find a way to a better life. Then Callum comes along and whisks her away to a whole new world. A world of privilege, excess, and people who are most likely to hug her with a smile while they stab her in the back and laugh. She's learned some valuable life lessons through all her hardship, though, and one thing she knows is that the fairytale is an illusion. Trust is something she doesn't know the meaning of.<br><br><b>This will never be my home. I don't belong in splendor, I belong in squalor. That's what I know. It's what I'm comfortable with because squalor doesn't lie to you. It's not wrapped up in a pretty package. It is what it is.</b><br><br>The five Royal boys are what I would describe as entitled teens with a god complex. Not only do they have power over their father, but they hold court as the monarchs of their private school. No one dares to question or cross them. Until Ella came to town. This was one of the most addictive parts of the story for me. Seeing this power struggle between Elle and the Lion's Den that she landed in. Though she had moments of intimidation, she never backed away from any of their challenges. She was witty, strong, and had an overall unique character with a fascinating personality. <br><br>If you're hoping for a hearts and flowers type of romance, you won't find that here. Reed can be downright despicable and intolerable at the best of times. He uses his mother's death as a free pass to cause havoc on anyone whom he sees fit. That being said, it didn't deter me one bit from the story as it played out in its grim glory. There were manipulations around every corner and I blissfully ate it up with a spoon. <br><br>All the power play between Ella and Reed developed into the kind of ripe sexual tension that readers dream of. It was positively decadent and made my heart flutter. It was <i>passionate</i>. <i>Thrilling.</i> It had my heart racing and turning the pages until I saw that tension reach its breaking point. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458231226i/18460075.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To sum things up, I was thoroughly ensconced in this glittering world of privilege and wealth. That glitter concealed a whole lot of depravity and sins. I took off half a point from my rating because of the events that occurred right before the cliffy. My jaw dropped and I was ready to kick Reed in his gold plated nuts. I'm really hoping that what happened wasn't what it appeared. (Though that seems pretty impossible)<br><br>Paper Princess was a far cry from your typical YA book, maybe that's one of the things I enjoyed about it the most. It was bold and brilliantly executed. Now after that horrendous cliffy, I'm just going to pretend that I don't have to wait until this summer to continue with the insanity with the Royals. I don't think I'll have the patience otherwise. <br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer5672499010604188627">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★<br/><br/><b>Now LIVE!<br/><a href='http://amzn.to/1Twjrxm' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> | <a href='http://amzn.to/1XchQvF' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459262443i/18588929._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I love these types of books, seriously they are my kryptonite, I can't get enough! High school, rich kids, angst, an arsehole hero, a feisty heroine, a little bit of smut. Yep, this is one of those books that makes this old bird a very happy woman.<br/><br/>17 year old Ella Harper has lived a very frugal life, and now she's all alone in the world without her beloved mother who recently passed away. She is trying to avoid the authorities and get on with her st</span>
  <span id="freeText5672499010604188627" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★<br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br><a href="http://amzn.to/1Twjrxm" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> | <a href="http://amzn.to/1XchQvF" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459262443i/18588929._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love these types of books, seriously they are my kryptonite, I can't get enough! High school, rich kids, angst, an arsehole hero, a feisty heroine, a little bit of smut. Yep, this is one of those books that makes this old bird a very happy woman.<br><br>17 year old Ella Harper has lived a very frugal life, and now she's all alone in the world without her beloved mother who recently passed away. She is trying to avoid the authorities and get on with her studies and hope like hell she can survive. That is until fate finally catches up with her and she is thrust into a world full of mean girls and arrogant boys.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"This will never be my home. I don't belong in splendor, I belong in squalor. That's what I know."</b>
</blockquote><br>Enter Callum Royal. He is a rich man with five sons. FIVE SONS! I want all of them to get a story, but I digress, he has five sons and when they discover that their father has won guardianship over a girl who is stripping for a living, it's safe to say they are not a happy bunch.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"If you stay, we’ll break you so bad that you’ll be crawling away."</b>
</blockquote><br>Reed Royal isn't the eldest son, but he's kinda the leader. He rules the school too, so what he says goes, and he does not trust this newcomer AT ALL.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459262443i/18588930._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is very heavy on the love/hate trope, and let me tell you these boys are mean! But as with any good book, the author slowly makes you fall in love and you can't help but be drawn in.<br><br>I cannot wait for more. A mature young adult novel that I recommend to anyone who likes bad boys and angst.<br><br>p.s Easton belongs to me ;)<br><br><b>Paper Princess is slated to be a trilogy, and does end rather shockingly! Told in dual POV.</b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><u>Images featured in this review were created by me using stock images either purchased from deposit photo or from free stock sites.</u><br><br><br>

<div id="review_1608184100" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608184100" />
    <a title="Andreea Pop" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop"><img alt="Andreea Pop" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486663526p2/4858513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1608184100?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andreea Pop" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andreea Pop" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop">Andreea Pop</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=brotherhood-for-the-ages">brotherhood-for-the-ages</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=non-fantasy">non-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=real-life-problems">real-life-problems</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=awesome-romance">awesome-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=amazing-feelings">amazing-feelings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=holy-shit">holy-shit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=swoon-worthy-characters">swoon-worthy-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1608184100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5409534810986411381"><i>Sorry, I just need to get this off my chest -- <b>THAT. FUCKING. CLIFFHANGER. </b><br/><br/><a href='https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-F_RVzq4IUr4/V5Ce_6KdKxI/AAAAAAAAQUQ/AVCaC66VoMQbQj90BrbWKcOVs8KE9M4bQCLcB/s1600/8038943.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'><img height='172' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469095769ra/19778893.gif' width='320' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Okay, I'll behave. Hopefully. </i><br/><br/><i>Paper Princess</i> is awesome in the distinct manner of being such an addictive, electrifying and soap-opera-ish novel. Truly, you need to take it as it is and you'll be destined for eternal love. Don't expect anything dazzling, it's still NA, and while NA can be deep and touching, it still has a vibe of entertainment purposes. It goes straight to the heart. And <i>Paper Princess</i> traps you in and do</span>
  <span id="freeText5409534810986411381" style="display:none"><i>Sorry, I just need to get this off my chest -- <b>THAT. FUCKING. CLIFFHANGER. </b><br><br><a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-F_RVzq4IUr4/V5Ce_6KdKxI/AAAAAAAAQUQ/AVCaC66VoMQbQj90BrbWKcOVs8KE9M4bQCLcB/s1600/8038943.gif" rel="nofollow noopener"><img height="172" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469095769ra/19778893.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Okay, I'll behave. Hopefully. </i><br><br><i>Paper Princess</i> is awesome in the distinct manner of being such an addictive, electrifying and soap-opera-ish novel. Truly, you need to take it as it is and you'll be destined for eternal love. Don't expect anything dazzling, it's still NA, and while NA can be deep and touching, it still has a vibe of entertainment purposes. It goes straight to the heart. And <i>Paper Princess</i> traps you in and doesn't let go. Seriously, it's 5AM. <br><br>The story is cliché-ish enough, but still -- loads of fun and loads of teen angst and loads of <i>Mean Girls</i> vibes and loads of sexy times and loads of bad boys and loads of this and that which make everything perfect in the end. Yeah, you're frustrated quite a lot, but it's so so satisfying. Does that make sense? <br><br>I did not expect to like it so much. I wanted something cute and fluffy and light, and although this book has all these qualities to a certain extent, one thing that distinguishes it from the ever-growing sea of contemporary titles is its fresh narrative that simply pulls you in. <br><br><a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WEJR6FLFeEA/V5Ce-NBvW-I/AAAAAAAAQUM/X0nYlNojV9ILxJEUrsHiQcHgtbSkPjrDACLcB/s1600/98712f3856f081d211bc3b0613a1e739.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="213" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469095769i/19778894.jpg" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Not gonna talk about the plot -- <i>shh, there isn't any honestly </i>-- read the synopsis and you're pretty much good to go; but you need to know a couple of things: Ella, badass chick, strength incarnate, optimist extraordinaire; the Royal brothers (5 of them, <b>IMAGINE THAT MUCH PHYSICAL PERFECTION</b>), fucking assholes, intense dudes, and goddamn lovable actually. Reed is a tough nut to crack but the essential is that you'll fall in love with him in no time. And while I do love him (most of the time), <b>EASTON IS MINEEEE.</b> Gah, I just realized I haven't fangirled so hard in a while. <br><br>I suppose I should mention the sizzling romance too since it'll most likely get everyone hot and bothered. Oh well, there's that. <i>Wowza wowza wowza hyperventilating-required stuff. </i><br><br><a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pQcDneeIWEY/V5Ce8wkgs0I/AAAAAAAAQUI/s3fKhiJZB2AVpvkndShHsli0Mj0uU-fZwCLcB/s1600/7fb4ebcc7408eb62a58a08ec2cfd0039.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469095769i/19778895.jpg" width="257" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Add high school drama, daddy issues, mommy issues, shit loads of money, forbidden feelings and FEELS and ta-daa you've got yourself a book. <br><br>On the other hand though, that ending pretty much killed me. I was expecting it -- everyone said it'd be brutal. <b>AND IT IS. <i>How???? Whyyy???</i></b> So many questions that I hope have some justifiable, clever, redeemable answers because I need the Royals to establish some peace in their household. <br><br>And the sequel comes out in a few days yassss bring on the juicy drama and sobs and pterodactyl screeches. <br><br><a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vxAlmmVAb9c/V5Ce_1_-aGI/AAAAAAAAQUU/DzckWMA-gzQrB3MzpFFj-dCjvaz2AwH0QCLcB/s1600/10339256.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="156" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469095769ra/19778896.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So yeah, go read it. If it hasn't been evident enough, I'll stress this further: <b>GO READ IT.</b> Go ahead, abandon yourself to the heartache! <i>*cackles maniacally*</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="5409534810986411381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1557441330" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1557441330" />
    <a title="S.M. West" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west"><img alt="S.M. West" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564323942p2/18424676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1557441330?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=i-m-an-angst-whore">i-m-an-angst-whore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=broken">broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=super-hot-bad-boy-badass">super-hot-bad-boy-badass</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=kickass-heroine">kickass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=sexy-as-fuck">sexy-as-fuck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=uber-sexy-hot-male-lead">uber-sexy-hot-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=sexy-athlete">sexy-athlete</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=top-25-of-2016">top-25-of-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1557441330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15780782286563985735"><b>5 STARS</b><br/><br/>What do you get when you meld together two brilliant storytellers, Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick - aka Erin Watt, and throw in similar feels to Cruel Intentions, Mean Girls and a Modern day Cinderella? <br/><a href='http://imgur.com/V2Vy8DH' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458794695ra/18530873.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I started this baby on a late night train home from a work thingy. I was exhausted and thought I’d just read a few chapters to unwind. By the time the train pulled into my station, I was like a junkie soaring from my last high and jonesing for my next hit! <br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/vEv75Xb' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458795560ra/18530931.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I rushed home, jumped in </span>
  <span id="freeText15780782286563985735" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS</b><br><br>What do you get when you meld together two brilliant storytellers, Elle Kennedy and Jen Frederick - aka Erin Watt, and throw in similar feels to Cruel Intentions, Mean Girls and a Modern day Cinderella? <br><a href="http://imgur.com/V2Vy8DH" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458794695ra/18530873.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I started this baby on a late night train home from a work thingy. I was exhausted and thought I’d just read a few chapters to unwind. By the time the train pulled into my station, I was like a junkie soaring from my last high and jonesing for my next hit! <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/vEv75Xb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458795560ra/18530931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I rushed home, jumped in bed and told myself I'd just read a few more chapters…until there were no more! Read the rest in one sitting. Sleep be damned! And yes, my sorry ass was tired the next morning <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/f96QIta" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458795560ra/18530932.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>but again, see above, I was freakin’ high as a kite and while I knew I'd eventually crash with one vicious book hangover, I didn’t care!<br><br>Ella Harper’s a 17 year old dynamo; I simply adored this girl for her spunk, resilient and take-no-prisoners attitude. Father’s unknown, mother’s passed away and no one knows that she’s on her own. She forged her mother’s signature on school documents, going to school during the day and has three jobs on the side, including stripping, to keep the lights on and to put food on the table. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/PP_zpsqjh1c3go.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458794695i/18530874._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo PP_zpsqjh1c3go.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then Callum Royal waltzes into her life, claiming he’s her guardian. He tells her that he’ll take care of her financially with enough money to go to college and beyond, and in return, she’ll live with him and his five boys. Ella’s carefully crafted life comes tumbling down around her. And then she meets the Royals and any remnants of life as she knew it is leveled. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/PP4_zpsla4rqrfm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458794695i/18530875.jpg" alt=" photo PP4_zpsla4rqrfm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>These boys don’t like her and the ring leader, Reed Royal, makes it known that she’s not welcomed and they won’t go easy on her. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/PP2_zps8dmfnelu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458794695i/18530876._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo PP2_zps8dmfnelu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ella gives as good as she gets. She was truly a formidable force for not only the Royals but also the psycho rich kids from Astor Park private school, who all take their cues on how to treat Ella from the Royals. Like Reed, all of them see her as a money grubbing whore and as such, she’s given the “royal” trash treatment.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/ujc1wv3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458794695ra/18530877.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Despite all the machinations and mind games, Ella can’t help but face that she’s attracted to Reed even though he’s the biggest asshole to her. You know the type. Reed’s the guy you love to hate and secretly lust after because let’s face it, he’s all alpha, dominant hotness. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Tnu4rUc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411868012ra/11292670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>“the apple is dangling in front of me, juicy red and delicious, but like the fairy tale, Reed Royal is the villain disguised as a pretty prince. Taking a bite out of him would be a huge mistake.”</b><br><br>Unbeknownst to Ella, Reed’s fighting the same fight. These two seriously held no punches and their fire and ice tango was tantalizing torture! <br><a href="http://imgur.com/tDTOnrG" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418622574ra/12851860.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Things escalate among Ella, those at school and the Royal boys, and as they reach a crescendo, Ella calls a truce. This is where things get even more interesting. It’s obvious that the Royals may be the “it” family but they’ve got dark secrets that they want to kept hidden. <br><br>I really liked each and every Royal...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/GkKMHKb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458794695ra/18530878.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>although, I think they all need some sort of redemption, including Daddy Royal. And I hope we get more. Something tells me that each of these boys would have great stories. Elle, Jen, are you listening? *hint, hint*!! <br><br>This story is rich with an intriguing, angst-ridden plot, complex characters that you can't help but FEEL something for and burning sexual tension between Reed and Ella that keeps you turning the pages. <br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/PP1_zpsihpmcb9r.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458794695i/18530879._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo PP1_zpsihpmcb9r.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And all of this culminates with one hellvua cliffhanger! WT??<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Ao6frlo" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423243435ra/13600164.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I highly recommend this book. If you want a movie like experience that'll give you so much and leave you hankering for more, you've got to read this!!</b><br><br>**ARC generously provided by authors in exchange for an honest review.**<br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts.</b> <br><br><a href="http://tiedupinromance.blogspot.be/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456487234i/18240613.png" width="400" height="148" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>-------<br><br>Upon finishing:<br></a><a href="http://imgur.com/TduZoxC" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458752117ra/18527034.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I seriously devoured this in one sitting and SH*T, now what the hell am I supposed to do? That CLIFFHANGER!!!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/frtLLNG" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458752117ra/18527035.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Don't know how I'm going to make it waiting for the next book!!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15780782286563985735" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('efjJ3FEbtyf7LCDRmH8ykT54KK8u18MD1dlknbgI2K6GBtTxX8H24C3wnRVvzCmtgs7RJQUE42xZzi0eCeC9Hg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NLeNiccgfPOSpTC6ZMugOba71y+0c66x+3obqtNymJbLSZCkyfo9NER5jX6TeLsFCg0upZ+gjt53bVIpYpr9Jg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
